<div class="wp-block-columns are-vertically-aligned-center newsletter-wrapper has-negro-azulado-background-color has-background is-layout-flex wp-container-core-columns-is-layout-774f1291 wp-block-columns-is-layout-flex" style="padding-top:50px;padding-right:50px;padding-bottom:50px;padding-left:40px">

<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-white-color has-text-color">Tu butaca en primera fila</h2>
